private_ownership_production_stocks = {
	every_scope_state = {

		################
		#building_food_industry
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_food_industry
				b:building_food_industry  = {
					private_ownership_fraction > 0.5
				}
				is_production_method_active = {
					building_type = building_food_industry
					production_method = pm_no_private_ownership_manufacture_stock
				}
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_food_industry
				production_method = pm_private_ownership_majority_manufacture_stock
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_food_industry
				b:building_food_industry  = {
					private_ownership_fraction <= 0.5
				}
				is_production_method_active = {
					building_type = building_food_industry
					production_method = pm_private_ownership_majority_manufacture_stock
				}
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_food_industry
				production_method = pm_no_private_ownership_manufacture_stock
			}
		}
		#building_textile_mills
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_textile_mills
				b:building_textile_mills  = {
					private_ownership_fraction > 0.5
				}
				is_production_method_active = {
					building_type = building_textile_mills
					production_method = pm_no_private_ownership_manufacture_stock
				}
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_textile_mills
				production_method = pm_private_ownership_majority_manufacture_stock
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_textile_mills
				b:building_textile_mills  = {
					private_ownership_fraction <= 0.5
				}
				is_production_method_active = {
					building_type = building_textile_mills
					production_method = pm_private_ownership_majority_manufacture_stock
				}
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_textile_mills
				production_method = pm_no_private_ownership_manufacture_stock
			}
		}
		#building_furniture_manufacturies
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_furniture_manufacturies
				b:building_furniture_manufacturies  = {
					private_ownership_fraction > 0.5
				}
				is_production_method_active = {
					building_type = building_furniture_manufacturies
					production_method = pm_no_private_ownership_manufacture_stock
				}
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_furniture_manufacturies
				production_method = pm_private_ownership_majority_manufacture_stock
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_furniture_manufacturies
				b:building_furniture_manufacturies  = {
					private_ownership_fraction <= 0.5
				}
				is_production_method_active = {
					building_type = building_furniture_manufacturies
					production_method = pm_private_ownership_majority_manufacture_stock
				}
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_furniture_manufacturies
				production_method = pm_no_private_ownership_manufacture_stock
			}
		}
		#building_glassworks
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_glassworks
				b:building_glassworks  = {
					private_ownership_fraction > 0.5
				}
				is_production_method_active = {
					building_type = building_glassworks
					production_method = pm_no_private_ownership_manufacture_stock
				}
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_glassworks
				production_method = pm_private_ownership_majority_manufacture_stock
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_glassworks
				b:building_glassworks  = {
					private_ownership_fraction <= 0.5
				}

fluctuations_country_indice_value_year = {
	change_variable = {
		name = index_value_count
		add = 1
	}

    if = {
        limit = {
            var:index_value_count = 1
        }
        set_variable = {
            name = country_indice_value_1
            value = country_indice
        }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            var:index_value_count = 2
        }
        set_variable = {
            name = country_indice_value_2
            value = country_indice
        }

        set_variable = {
            name = country_indice_value_dif_01
            value = 0
        }
        change_variable = {
            name = country_indice_value_dif_01
            add = var:country_indice_value_2
        }
        change_variable = {
            name = country_indice_value_dif_01
            subtract = var:country_indice_value_1
        }
        change_variable = {
            name = country_indice_value_dif_01
            divide = var:country_indice_value_1
        }

		#change base_index_value
		set_variable = {
			name = base_index_value_dif
			value = var:base_index_value
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = base_index_value_dif
			multiply = var:country_indice_value_dif_01
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				or = {
					var:base_index_value < 1000000 #point
					base_index_value_dif < 0
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = base_index_value
				add = var:base_index_value_dif
			}
		}

        set_variable = {
            name = index_value_count
            value = 0
        }

		if = {
			limit = {
				var:country_indice_value_dif_01 < -0.5
			}
			financial_crash = yes
		}
    }
}
fluctuations_country_indice_value_year_clear = {
	set_variable = {
		name = country_indice_value_dif_01
		value = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = base_index_value_dif
		value = 0
	}
}

#########################################################################################################################################################################################
#########################################################################################################################################################################################

#

#########################################################################################################################################################################################
#########################################################################################################################################################################################
#########################################################################################################################################################################################
#########################################################################################################################################################################################

central_bank_production_methods = {
	every_scope_state = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner  = {
					national_debt_compared_gdp >= 0.05
				}
				is_production_method_active = {
					building_type = building_bank
					production_method = pm_no_bond_production
				}
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_bank
				production_method = pm_bond_production
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner  = {
					national_debt_compared_gdp < 0.05
				}
				is_production_method_active = {
					building_type = building_bank
					production_method = pm_bond_production
				}
			}
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_bank
				production_method = pm_no_bond_production
			}
		}
	}
}

#########################################################################################################################################################################################

buy_bond_in_currrency_var = {
	every_scope_state = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
				is_capital = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = central_bank_site
		}
	}

	scope:seller = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_law = law_type:law_dinar_currency
			}
			scope:buyer = {
				scope:central_bank_site = {

# has_modifier = has_financial_center

# 	has_modifier = economic_instability
# }

currency_crisis = {
	#objectif:
	# - la devise baisse de 50% -> les pays étranger perde la confiance -> revente massive de la devise -> inflation scripter qui calcule la différence excte de valeur etre les 2 extreme de valeur
	# - revente integrale de la devise possedé par les pays étranger
	# - control des change pour ne pas etre acheter
	# - blocage des route de commerce

	capital= {
		save_scope_as = capital_state
	}
	save_scope_as = target_country

	set_variable = {
		name = currency_crisis
		value = 1
	}

	country_credit_rating = yes
	#event for player
	if = {
		limit  = {
			is_subject_custom_trigger = no
			is_revolutionary =  no
			has_modifier = has_central_bank
			# not = {
			# 	has_modifier = economic_instability
			# }
			or = {
				is_at_war = yes
				var:economic_instability_count >= 1
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = 00_ef_economic_instability_event.1
				days = 0
				popup = no
			}
		}
	}
	economic_instability = yes
}
economic_crisis = {
	capital= {
		save_scope_as = capital_state
	}
	save_scope_as = target_country

	set_variable = {
		name = economic_crisis
		value = 1
	}

	country_credit_rating = yes
	#event for player
	if = {
		limit  = {
			#is_subject_custom_trigger = no
			is_revolutionary =  no
			global_country_ranking < 100  #all pays
			#has_modifier = has_central_bank
			# not = {
			# 	has_modifier = economic_instability
			# }
			or = {
				is_at_war = yes
				var:economic_instability_count >= 1
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = 00_ef_economic_instability_event.2
				days = 0
				popup = no
			}
		}
	}
	economic_instability = yes
} #-> revante devise en mass + pas de rachat si foreign_exchange_controls

country_bankruptcy = {
	capital= {
		save_scope_as = capital_state
	}
	save_scope_as = target_country

	set_variable = {
		name = country_bankruptcy
		value = 1
	}

	country_credit_rating = yes
	#event for player
	if = {
		limit  = {
			is_subject_custom_trigger = no
			is_revolutionary =  no
			global_country_ranking < 50 #all pays
			# not = {
			# 	has_modifier = economic_instability
			# }
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = 00_ef_economic_instability_event.5
				days = 0
				popup = no
			}
		}
	}
	economic_instability = yes
}
########################################################################################

economic_instability = {

	########################################################################################
	# #test
	# set_variable = {
	# 	name = country_indice_value_dif_01
	# 	value = -0.6
	# }
	########################################################################################

	root = {
		save_scope_as = target_country
	}
	#Country Bankrupt - ok

	#event: ? si déclanche grace au trigger

	#Bank central Bankrupt = weak currency - ok
	#Crise monetaire = currency crisis (diminution de la valeur de la devise de plus de 50%/) -> délock l'inflation -> création d'inflation dans le monetary policy -> crise inflationniste du a la dette à vopitr
	#Crise économique =  Economic crisis (diminution de la valeur du PIB de plus de 50%)
	#Crash financier = Financial crash (diminution de la valeur de l'index des marché de plus de 50%)

		#pour le modifier economic_instability les pays sont vendeur sur la devise meme en dehor d'une crise de la dvise


	##############
	#General
	##############

	#perte de prestige 25% voir plus
	#malus diplomatique avec tout les pays uniquement si default sur dette

	##############
	#evenement spe
	##############

	change_variable = {
		name = economic_instability_count
		add = 1
	}

	#economic_instability notif
	if = {
		limit  = {
			var:economic_instability_count = 1
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
				not = {
					or  = {
						is_at_war = yes
						is_revolutionary = yes
						var:country_bankruptcy = 1
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = 00_ef_economic_instability_event.6
				days = 0
				popup = no
			}
		}
	}

	#economic_instability concequences
	if = {
		limit  = {
			or  = {
				var:economic_instability_count >= 2
				is_at_war = yes
				is_revolutionary = yes
				var:country_bankruptcy >= 1
			}
		}

		#country_bankruptcy
		if = {
			limit  = {
				var:country_bankruptcy >= 1
				not = {
					has_modifier = declared_bankruptcy
				}
			}

			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BBB
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BB
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_B
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CCC
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CC
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_C
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
			add_modifier = {
				name = country_credit_rating_C
			}

			remove_modifier = economic_instability
			add_modifier = {
				name = economic_instability
				months = 23
			}

			# remove_modifier = modifierr vanila
			# add_modifier = {
			# 	name = modifierr vanila
			# 	months = 23
			# }
		}

		# currency_crisis/central_bank_bankruptcy
		if = {
			limit  = {
				or = {
					var:currency_crisis >= 1
					var:central_bank_bankruptcy >= 1
				}
				not = {
					or = {
						has_modifier = central_bank_bankruptcy_country
						has_modifier = currency_crisis_country
					}
				}
			}
			remove_modifier = foreign_exchange_controls
			add_modifier = {
				name = foreign_exchange_controls
				months = 23
			}

			if = {
				limit  = {
					has_modifier = has_central_bank
				}
				every_country = {
					if = {
						limit  = {
							has_modifier = has_central_bank
							not = {
								this = root
								is_subject = yes
							}
						}
						save_scope_as = seller
						all_currency_resold = yes
					}
				}
			}
			#-> création d'hyper inflation scripté

			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BBB
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BB
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_B
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CCC
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CC
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_C
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
			add_modifier = {
				name = country_credit_rating_D
				#-> blocage des route de commerce qui devrai rester grace au extreme weak currency (pas besoins d'un modificateur siupplémentaire)
				#-> nécessité d'atribué le extrem weak currency oui ou non ?
			}

			remove_modifier = economic_instability
			add_modifier = {
				name = economic_instability
				months = 23
			}
			if = {
				limit  = {
					var:central_bank_bankruptcy = 1
				}
				remove_modifier = central_bank_bankruptcy_country
				add_modifier = {
					name = central_bank_bankruptcy_country
					months = 23
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit  = {
					var:currency_crisis = 1
				}
				remove_modifier = currency_crisis_country
				add_modifier = {
					name = currency_crisis_country
					months = 23
				}
			}
		}

		#financial_crash
		if = {
			limit  = {
				var:financial_crash >= 1
				not = {
					has_modifier = financial_crash_country
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit  = {
					# not = {
					# 	is_subject = yes
					# }
					has_modifier = has_central_bank
					has_modifier = has_financial_center
				}
				financial_crash_consequences = yes
			}

			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BBB
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BB
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_B
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CCC
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CC
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_C
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
			add_modifier = {
				name = country_credit_rating_CC
			}

			remove_modifier = economic_instability
			add_modifier = {
				name = economic_instability #bloc l'achat de  la devise et favorrise sa vente / bloc le base ratre à 10%
				months = 23
			}
			remove_modifier = financial_crash_country
			add_modifier = {
				name = financial_crash_country
				multiplier = var:country_indice_value_dif_01
				months = 23
			}
		}

		#economic_crisis
		if = {
			limit  = {
				var:economic_crisis >= 1
				not = {
					has_modifier = economic_crisis_country
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit  = {
					# not = {
					# 	is_subject = yes
					# }
					has_modifier = has_central_bank
					has_modifier = has_financial_center
				}
				economic_crisis_consequences = yes
			}

			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BBB
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_BB
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_B
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CCC
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_CC
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_C
			remove_modifier = country_credit_rating_D
			add_modifier = {
				name = country_credit_rating_C
			}

			remove_modifier = economic_instability
			add_modifier = {
				name = economic_instability #bloc l'achat de  la devise et favorrise sa vente / bloc le base ratre à 10%
				months = 23
			}
			remove_modifier = economic_crisis_country
			add_modifier = {
				name = economic_crisis_country
				months = 23
			}
		}
	}
}

financial_crash_consequences = {

	financial_crash_destroy_financial_center = yes

	#perte de capital du privé
	change_variable = {
		name = government_loan
		subtract = investor_massive_capital_loss
	}
	add_investment_pool = investor_massive_capital_loss

	#faillite des entreprise
	bankrupt_company = yes #-> à revoir

	#faillite batiment privé
	every_scope_building = {
		limit = {
			or = {
				#financial center
				is_building_type = building_financial_centre
				is_building_type = building_financial_centre_fra
				is_building_type = building_financial_centre_gbr
				is_building_type = building_financial_centre_usa
				is_building_type = building_financial_centre_net
				is_building_type = building_financial_centre_ger
				is_building_type = building_financial_centre_aus
				is_building_type = building_financial_centre_ita
				is_building_type = building_financial_centre_chi
				is_building_type = building_financial_centre_jap

				#manuf
				is_building_type = building_food_industry
				is_building_type = building_textile_mills
				is_building_type = building_furniture_manufacturies
				is_building_type = building_glassworks
				is_building_type = building_tooling_workshops
				is_building_type = building_paper_mills
				is_building_type = building_chemical_plants
				is_building_type = building_explosives_factory
				is_building_type = building_synthetics_plants
				is_building_type = building_steel_mills
				is_building_type = building_motor_industry
				is_building_type = building_shipyards
				is_building_type = building_military_shipyards
				is_building_type = building_war_machine_industry
				is_building_type = building_electrics_industry
				is_building_type = building_arms_industry
				is_building_type = building_artillery_foundries
				is_building_type = building_munition_plants

				#farm plantation
				is_building_type = building_rye_farm
				is_building_type = building_wheat_farm
				is_building_type = building_rice_farm
				is_building_type = building_maize_farm
				is_building_type = building_millet_farm
				is_building_type = building_livestock_ranch
				is_building_type = building_vineyard_plantation
				is_building_type = building_logging_camp
				is_building_type = building_rubber_plantation
				is_building_type = building_fishing_wharf
				is_building_type = building_whaling_station
				is_building_type = building_coffee_plantation
				is_building_type = building_cotton_plantation
				is_building_type = building_dye_plantation
				is_building_type = building_opium_plantation
				is_building_type = building_tea_plantation
				is_building_type = building_tobacco_plantation
				is_building_type = building_sugar_plantation
				is_building_type = building_banana_plantation
				is_building_type = building_silk_plantation
				is_building_type = building_vineyard_plantation

				#mine
				is_building_type = building_coal_mine
				is_building_type = building_iron_mine
				is_building_type = building_lead_mine
				is_building_type = building_sulfur_mine
				is_building_type = building_oil_rig

				#railway
				is_building_type = building_railway
			}
			private_ownership_fraction > 0.5
		}
		remove_modifier = financial_crash
		add_modifier = {
			name = financial_crash
			months = 23
		}
	}
}
economic_crisis_consequences = {

	economic_crisis_destroy_central_bank = yes

	#perte de capital des pop
	change_variable = {
		name = government_loan
		subtract = pop_capital_loss
	}
	change_variable = {
		name = pop_capital_loss_fix
		add = pop_capital_loss
	}

	#faillite des entreprise
	bankrupt_company = yes #-> à revoir

	#faillite batiment privé et publique
	every_scope_building = {
		limit = {
			or = {
				#admin

			months = 23
